Typically hard money lenders will lend 50-70% of the value of the property regardless of the sales price (unlike banks). The first step of the foreclosure process (which typically takes a number of months) that the lender will take is to file the notice of default. This is a public document that is recorded.\r\n* Tax liens - Each state creates the system and rules for the lien or deed process so careful research is necessary.
